(******************************************************************************************

 Whiskered bifunctors

 In this file, we define whiskered bifunctors for enriched categories. These represent
 functors from the tensor of two enriched categories to another enriched category. We use
 a whiskered style in this definition meaning that we have a left action and a right action
 rather than a single action.

 Let's be more concrete. In a curried bifunctor, we have for all `x₁ x₂ : C₁` and `y₁ y₂ : C₂`
 a morphism `E₁ ⦃ x₁ , x₂ ⦄ ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁ , y₂ ⦄) --> E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁ , F x₂ y₂ ⦄`. For a whiskered
 bifunctor, we split this into two morphisms:
 - a left action `E₁ ⦃ x₁ , x₂ ⦄ --> E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y , F x₂ y ⦄`
 - a right action `E₂ ⦃ y₁ , y₂ ⦄ --> E₃ ⦃ F x y₁ , F x y₂ ⦄`
 The advantage of this definition over the others, is that the laws become simpler. The
 reason for that comes from the composition operation of the tensor of two enriched categories.
 For that operation, we use the so-called `inner_swap` morphism, which gives us a morphism
 from `(E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄ ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄ ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))` to the object
 `(E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄ ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄ ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))` where the two middle
 objects are swapped. This `inner_swap` morphism has a rather complicated definition. By
 using the whiskered style, the laws become much simpler. In the definition of the laws
 ([enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_laws]), one can see that none uses `inner_swap`, and that
 no associators/unitors are present (only one braiding).

 Contents
 1. Definition of whiskered bifunctors
 2. Accessors for whiskered bifunctors
 3. Equivalence with functors from the tensor

 ******************************************************************************************)

(** * 1. Definition of whiskered bifunctors *)
Definition enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data
           {V : monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           (E₁ : enrichment C₁ V)
           (E₂ : enrichment C₂ V)
           (E₃ : enrichment C₃ V)
  : UU
  := ∑ (F : C₁ → C₂ → C₃),
     (∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁)
        (y : C₂),
      E₁ ⦃ x₁ , x₂ ⦄
      -->
      E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y , F x₂ y ⦄)
     ×
     (∏ (x : C₁)
        (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
      E₂ ⦃ y₁ , y₂ ⦄
      -->
      E₃ ⦃ F x y₁ , F x y₂ ⦄).

Definition make_enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data
           {V : monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
           {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
           {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
           (F : C₁ → C₂ → C₃)
           (Fl : ∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁)
                   (y : C₂),
                 E₁ ⦃ x₁ , x₂ ⦄
                 -->
                 E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y , F x₂ y ⦄)
           (Fr : ∏ (x : C₁)
                   (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
                 E₂ ⦃ y₁ , y₂ ⦄
                 -->
                 E₃ ⦃ F x y₁ , F x y₂ ⦄)
  : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃
  := F ,, Fl ,, Fr.

Definition enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_ob
           {V : monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
           {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
           {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
           (F : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃)
           (x : C₁)
           (y : C₂)
  : C₃
  := pr1 F x y.

Coercion enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_ob : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data >-> Funclass.

Definition enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
           {V : monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
           {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
           {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
           (F : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃)
           (x₁ x₂ : C₁)
           (y : C₂)
  : E₁ ⦃ x₁ , x₂ ⦄
    -->
    E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y , F x₂ y ⦄
  := pr12 F x₁ x₂ y.

Definition enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
           {V : monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
           {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
           {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
           (F : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃)
           (x : C₁)
           (y₁ y₂ : C₂)
  : E₂ ⦃ y₁ , y₂ ⦄
    -->
    E₃ ⦃ F x y₁ , F x y₂ ⦄
  := pr22 F x y₁ y₂.

Definition enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_laws
           {V : sym_monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
           {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
           {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
           (F : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃)
  : UU
  := (∏ (x : C₁) (y : C₂),
      enriched_id E₁ x · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y
      =
      enriched_id E₃ (F x y))
     ×
     (∏ (x : C₁) (y : C₂),
      enriched_id E₂ y · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y
      =
      enriched_id E₃ (F x y))
     ×
     (∏ (x₁ x₂ x₃ : C₁) (y : C₂),
      enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃ · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₃ y
      =
      (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₂ x₃ y
       #⊗
       enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y) (F x₂ y) (F x₃ y))
     ×
     (∏ (x : C₁) (y₁ y₂ y₃ : C₂),
      enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃ · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₁ y₃
      =
      (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₂ y₃
       #⊗
       enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₁ y₂)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y₁) (F x y₂) (F x y₃))
     ×
     (∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
      enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
      #⊗
      enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
      · enriched_comp _ _ _ _
      =
      sym_mon_braiding V _ _
      ·
      (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F _ _ _
       #⊗
       enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F _ _ _)
      · enriched_comp _ _ _ _).


V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃
isaprop (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_laws F)


V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃
isaprop (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_laws F)

  repeat (use isapropdirprod) ; repeat (use impred ; intro) ; apply homset_property.
Qed.

Definition enriched_whiskered_bifunctor
           {V : sym_monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           (E₁ : enrichment C₁ V)
           (E₂ : enrichment C₂ V)
           (E₃ : enrichment C₃ V)
  : UU
  := ∑ (F : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃),
     enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_laws F.

Definition make_enriched_whiskered_bifunctor
           {V : sym_monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
           {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
           {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
           (F : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃)
           (HF : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_laws F)
  : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
  := F ,, HF.


V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃


V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃

  exact (pr1 F).
Defined.

(** * 2. Accessors for whiskered bifunctors *)
Section Accessors.
  Context {V : sym_monoidal_cat}
          {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
          {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
          {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
          {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
          (F : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃).

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y: C₂
enriched_id E₁ x
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y: C₂
enriched_id E₁ x
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

    exact (pr12 F x y).
  Defined.

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y: C₂
enriched_id E₂ y
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y: C₂
enriched_id E₂ y
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

    exact (pr122 F x y).
  Defined.

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y: C₂
enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₃ y =
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₂ x₃ y
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y) (F x₂ y) (F x₃ y)

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y: C₂
enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₃ y =
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₂ x₃ y
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y) (F x₂ y) (F x₃ y)

    exact (pr1 (pr222 F) x₁ x₂ x₃ y).
  Defined.

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₁ y₃ =
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₂ y₃
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x y₁) (F x y₂) (F x y₃)

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₁ y₃ =
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₂ y₃
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x y₁) (F x y₂) (F x y₃)

    exact (pr12 (pr222 F) x y₁ y₂ y₃).
  Defined.

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂)

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂)

    exact (pr22 (pr222 F) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂).
  Defined.

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V

#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂)

#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) =

· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂)

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V

E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁

enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
   #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V

x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
     #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂)

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) =
identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂)

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) =
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₁ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₁
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂)

    apply idpath.
  Qed.
End Accessors.

(** * 3. Equivalence with functors from the tensor *)
Section FromWhiskeredBifunctor.
  Context {V : sym_monoidal_cat}
          {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
          {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
          {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
          {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
          (F : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃).

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_curried_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_curried_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
C₁ → C₂ → C₃
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
V ⟦ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄),
E₃ ⦃ ?F x₁ y₁, ?F x₂ y₂ ⦄ ⟧

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
C₁ → C₂ → C₃
 exact (λ x y, F x y).
    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
V ⟦ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄),
E₃ ⦃ (λ (x : C₁) (y : C₂), F x y) x₁ y₁,
(λ (x : C₁) (y : C₂), F x y) x₂ y₂ ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂,
             enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
             #⊗
             enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
             · enriched_comp _ _ _ _).
  Defined.

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_curried_bifunctor_laws
  enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_curried_bifunctor_laws
  enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x : C₁) (y : C₂),
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor
    enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x x y
    y =
enriched_id E₃
  (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x y)
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ x₃ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ y₃ : C₂),
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor
    enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₁ x₃
    y₁ y₃ =
enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor
  enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₂ x₃
  y₂ y₃
#⊗ enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor
     enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₁
     x₂ y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃
    (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₁
       y₁)
    (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₂
       y₂)
    (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₃
       y₃)

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x : C₁) (y : C₂),
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor
    enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x x y
    y =
enriched_id E₃
  (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x y)
 
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y: C₂
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y
· (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y
   #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y)) =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y: C₂
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· (enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y
   · (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y
      #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y))) =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category

mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· (enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y
   · (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y
      #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y))) =
?b
V: sym_monoidal_cat

x: C₁

?b = enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

mon_linvunitor I_{ V}

   · (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y
      #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y))) =
?b

enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y

   #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y)) = ?t2

  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y) = ?t2

        
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category

enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y = 
?y'

        
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y: C₂
(enriched_id E₁ x
 · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x x y)
#⊗ (enriched_id E₂ y
    · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y) =
?y'

enriched_id E₃ (F x y)
#⊗ (enriched_id E₂ y
    · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x y y) =
?y'

        
V: sym_monoidal_cat

x: C₁
y: C₂
enriched_id E₃ (F x y) #⊗ enriched_id E₃ (F x y) = ?y'

        apply idpath.
      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V

x: C₁
y: C₂
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· (enriched_id E₃ (F x y) #⊗ enriched_id E₃ (F x y)
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y)) =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V

x: C₁
y: C₂
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· (identity I_{ V} #⊗ enriched_id E₃ (F x y)
   · enriched_id E₃ (F x y)
     #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x y, F x y ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y)) =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category

x: C₁
y: C₂
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· (identity I_{ V} #⊗ enriched_id E₃ (F x y)
   · (enriched_id E₃ (F x y)
      #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x y, F x y ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x y) (F x y) (F x y))) =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category

mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· (identity I_{ V} #⊗ enriched_id E₃ (F x y)
   · mon_lunitor (E₃ ⦃ F x y, F x y ⦄)) =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat

y: C₂
mon_linvunitor I_{ V}
· (mon_lunitor I_{ V} · enriched_id E₃ (F x y)) =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat

x: C₁
y: C₂
mon_linvunitor I_{ V} · mon_lunitor I_{ V}
· enriched_id E₃ (F x y) = enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V

E₃: enrichment C₃ V

x: C₁
y: C₂
identity I_{ V} · enriched_id E₃ (F x y) =
enriched_id E₃ (F x y)

      apply id_left.
    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ x₃ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ y₃ : C₂),
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor
    enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₁ x₃
    y₁ y₃ =
enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor
  enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₂ x₃
  y₂ y₃
#⊗ enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor
     enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₁
     x₂ y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃
    (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₁
       y₁)
    (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₂
       y₂)
    (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried_data x₃
       y₃)
 
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₃ y₃
   #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₃
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)) =
(enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₂ x₃ y₃
 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₂ y₃
 · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₂ y₂) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))
#⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
    #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
    · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂))
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) (F x₃ y₃)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
   #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
   · (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₃ y₃
      #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₃
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))) =
(enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₂ x₃ y₃
 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₂ y₃
 · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₂ y₂) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))
#⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
    #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
    · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂))
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) (F x₃ y₃)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
   #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
   · (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₃ y₃
      #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₃
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))) =
?b
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
?b =
(enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₂ x₃ y₃
 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₂ y₃
 · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₂ y₂) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))
#⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
    #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₁ y₂
    · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂))
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) (F x₃ y₃)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V

      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))) =
?b

      #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
           (F x₂ y₂))
· identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃) = 
?t2

          apply idpath.
        
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
(identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₂ y₂ y₃)
#⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₂
    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₂, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
     ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₂ y₂ ⦄)
      ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
   · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     #⊗ (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₂, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
         #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
              (F x₂ y₂))
   · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)) =
?b

V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
   #⊗ (mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
         (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
       · ((sym_mon_braiding V (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
             (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
           · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂
               y₃
             #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F
                  x₁ y₂ y₃
           · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃)
               (F x₂ y₃))
          #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
          · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
              (F x₂ y₃)))
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)) =
(identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₂ y₃)
#⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₃
    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (inner_swap V (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
   · (enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)
      #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
           (F x₁ y₃)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)))

  (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
   #⊗ mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
        (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)

               y₃
             #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F
                  x₁ y₂ y₃
           · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃)
               (F x₂ y₃))
          #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
      · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
        #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
             (F x₂ y₃))
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)) =

      #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
           (F x₁ y₃)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)))

     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄))
#⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄) = ?y'

        apply idpath.
      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
   #⊗ mon_rassociator (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
        (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
   · (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
      #⊗ ((enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₂
             y₃
           #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁
                x₂ y₃
           · sym_mon_braiding V
               (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
               (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄))
          #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
          · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃)
              (F x₂ y₃)
            #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
      · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
        #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
             (F x₂ y₃)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))) =
(identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₂ y₃)
#⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₃
    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (inner_swap V (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
   · (enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)
      #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
           (F x₁ y₃)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)))

  (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)

   #⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₂ y₃

     #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)

    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)))

  (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

       · mon_rassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
           (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
           (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
       · sym_mon_braiding V (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
           (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
         #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
       · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃)
           (F x₂ y₃)
         #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
   · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)) =
?b
V: sym_monoidal_cat

E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃

y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
?b =
(identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₂ y₃)
#⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₃
    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (inner_swap V (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
   · (enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)
      #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
           (F x₁ y₃)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)))

 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₂ y₃)

    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

      #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

 #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right F x₁ y₂ y₃)
#⊗ (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y₃
    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

      #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
            (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
          #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

         #⊗ (enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃)
               (F x₂ y₃)
             #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

  (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· (enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)
   #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃)
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))

            #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
                 (F x₂ y₃)
            · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃)
                (F x₃ y₃))))) =
mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
  ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
   ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms V
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
      ⊗ ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
         ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)))
     ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
      ⊗ ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
         ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)))
     (mon_rassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
        (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
        (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
      · (rightwhiskering_on_morphisms V
           (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
           ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
            ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄))
           ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
            ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄))
           (sym_mon_braiding V
              (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
              (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄))
         · mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
             (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
             (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)))
   · mon_rassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
       (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
       ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
        ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)))
· (enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃)
   #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃)
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))

            (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
          #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

      #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)

      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))) =
?b

     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· (mon_rassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
     ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
      ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
   · (mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
        (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
        ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
         ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
      · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
        #⊗ (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
            #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
                 (F x₁ y₃))
      · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
        #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃)
             (F x₂ y₃)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))) =

   #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₃) (F x₃ y₃))

  (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
  ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
   ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· (mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
     ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
      ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
   · (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
      #⊗ (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
          #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
               (F x₁ y₃))
      · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
        #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃)
             (F x₂ y₃))) = ?t2

        
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
mon_rassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
  ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
   ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
    (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
    ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
     ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
      #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
           (F x₁ y₃))
· identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃) =
?t2

identity
  ((E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
   ⊗ ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
      ⊗ ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
         ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))))
· identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
      #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
           (F x₁ y₃))

  #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃) =

        apply idpath.

x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁

identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_lassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
     (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
   #⊗ (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
       #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
            (F x₁ y₃))
   · identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
     #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃)) =
identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
#⊗ (enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃)
    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))
· identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)

      (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
      (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
    · (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
       #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂)
            (F x₁ y₃)
       · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃)
           (F x₂ y₃))) =
identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₂ y₃, F x₃ y₃ ⦄)
#⊗ (enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃)
    #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
    · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃))

  (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄) (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
   #⊗ enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃)
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃)) =
enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃)
#⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)

  (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄) (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· mon_rassociator (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
    (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
    (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃)
  #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃) =
enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₂) (F x₁ y₃) (F x₂ y₃)
#⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)

identity
  ((E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₃, F x₂ y₃ ⦄)
   ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₂, F x₁ y₃ ⦄)
   ⊗ (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄))

  #⊗ identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y₁, F x₁ y₂ ⦄)

· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)

· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₃)

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

Section ToWhiskeredBifunctor.
  Context {V : sym_monoidal_cat}
          {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
          {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
          {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
          {E₃ : enrichment C₃ V}
          (F : enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃).

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃

E₃: enrichment C₃ V

enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_data E₁ E₂ E₃

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat

E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
C₁ → C₂ → C₃
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y : C₂),
V ⟦ E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄, E₃ ⦃ ?F x₁ y, ?F x₂ y ⦄ ⟧
V: sym_monoidal_cat

E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V

F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
V ⟦ E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄, E₃ ⦃ ?F x y₁, ?F x y₂ ⦄ ⟧

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
C₁ → C₂ → C₃
 exact (λ x y, F x y).
    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y : C₂),
V ⟦ E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄,
E₃ ⦃ (λ (x : C₁) (y0 : C₂), F x y0) x₁ y,
(λ (x : C₁) (y0 : C₂), F x y0) x₂ y ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ x₁ x₂ y,
             mon_rinvunitor _
             · (identity _ #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y)
             · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y y).
    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
V ⟦ E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄,
E₃ ⦃ (λ (x0 : C₁) (y : C₂), F x0 y) x y₁,
(λ (x0 : C₁) (y : C₂), F x0 y) x y₂ ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ x y₁ y₂,
             mon_linvunitor _
             · (enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ identity _)
             · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x x y₁ y₂).
  Defined.

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_laws
  enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat

E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_laws
  enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x : C₁) (y : C₂),
enriched_id E₁ x
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
    enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x x y =
enriched_id E₃
  (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y)
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x : C₁) (y : C₂),
enriched_id E₂ y
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
    enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y y =
enriched_id E₃
  (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y)
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ x₃ : C₁) (y : C₂),
enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
    enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ x₃ y =
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
  enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ x₃ y
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
     enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ x₂ y
· enriched_comp E₃
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₃ y)
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x : C₁) (y₁ y₂ y₃ : C₂),
enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
    enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y₁ y₃ =
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
  enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y₂ y₃
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
     enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y₁)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y₂)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y₃)
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
  enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ x₂ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
     enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y₁
     y₂
· enriched_comp E₃
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y₁)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y₂)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
    enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y₁ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
       enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ x₂
       y₁
· enriched_comp E₃
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y₁)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y₁)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y₂)

E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x : C₁) (y : C₂),
enriched_id E₁ x
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
    enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x x y =
enriched_id E₃
  (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y)

    · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y)

    (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y, y ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃ #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y y y =
enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
· mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₃ ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₃ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y

· (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y)

· identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ (mon_lunitor I_{ V} · enriched_id E₂ y) = ?t2

        apply idpath.
      
V: sym_monoidal_cat

E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· (inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) I_{ V} (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
     I_{ V}
   · (enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
      #⊗ identity (I_{ V} ⊗ I_{ V})
      · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₃ ⦄)
        #⊗ (mon_lunitor I_{ V} · enriched_id E₂ y))) =
enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₃
· (mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₃ ⦄)
   · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₃ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y)

  I_{ V}
· leftwhiskering_on_morphisms V
    ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))
    (I_{ V} ⊗ I_{ V}) I_{ V} (mon_lunitor I_{ V})
· mon_runitor ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))

        
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂, x₃: C₁
y: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) I_{ V} (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  I_{ V}
· (identity ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))
   #⊗ mon_lunitor I_{ V}
   · mon_runitor ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))) =
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) I_{ V} (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  I_{ V}
· (leftwhiskering_on_morphisms V
     ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))
     (I_{ V} ⊗ I_{ V}) I_{ V} (mon_lunitor I_{ V})
   · mon_runitor ((E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)))

    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y₁)

    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x y₃)

E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· ((enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄))
   #⊗ (enriched_id E₁ x #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
   · (inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x, x ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
        (E₁ ⦃ x, x ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₁ x x x
        #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃)) = ?b

· mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₃ ⦄)

C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· inner_swap V I_{ V} (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) I_{ V}
    (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· identity (I_{ V} ⊗ I_{ V})
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃
· mon_runitor I_{ V} #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₃ ⦄) =
mon_linvunitor ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· identity I_{ V} #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₃

V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =
identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

x: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
(mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄)
 · mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄))
#⊗ (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)) =
identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

x: C₁
y₁, y₂, y₃: C₂
identity (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =
identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

identity ((E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₃ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

      apply idpath.
    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
∏ (x₁ x₂ : C₁) (y₁ y₂ : C₂),
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
  enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ x₂ y₂
#⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
     enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y₁
     y₂
· enriched_comp E₃
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y₁)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y₂)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_right
    enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y₁ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left
       enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ x₂
       y₁
· enriched_comp E₃
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₁ y₁)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y₁)
    (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered_data x₂ y₂)
 
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
(mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
 · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂
 · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₂ y₂)
#⊗ (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₁ y₁ y₂)
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · enriched_id E₁ x₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₂ x₂ y₁ y₂)
  #⊗ (mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
      · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₁
      · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁ y₁)
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂)



      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂)
  #⊗ (enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₂ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₁ y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   #⊗ mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
   · (enriched_id E₁ x₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
     #⊗ (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₁)
   · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₂ x₂ y₁ y₂
     #⊗ enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁ y₁)
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁) (F x₂ y₂)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V

E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· ((identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂)
   #⊗ (enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
   · (enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₂ y₂
      #⊗ enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₁ y₁ y₂
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂))) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   #⊗ mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
   · ((enriched_id E₁ x₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
      #⊗ (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
          #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₁)
      · (enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₂ x₂ y₁ y₂
         #⊗ enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁
              y₁
         · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₂ y₁)
             (F x₂ y₂))))

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V

x₁, x₂: C₁

mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· ((identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂)
   #⊗ (enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
   · (inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₂ ⦄)
        (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂
        #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂
      · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂)) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   #⊗ mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
   · ((enriched_id E₁ x₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
      #⊗ (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
          #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₁)
      · (inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
           (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₁ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₂
           #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₁ y₂
         · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁
             y₂)))

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category

x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂)
  #⊗ (enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₂ ⦄)
    (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· (enriched_id E₁ x₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
  #⊗ (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₁)
· inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₁ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₂
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₁ y₂
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂

V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₁ x₁)
  #⊗ (enriched_id E₂ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂ = ?t2

        
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· ((identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₁ x₁)
   #⊗ (enriched_id E₂ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
   · enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂
     #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂) = ?t2

V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
     (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)) =
sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   #⊗ mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
   · ((enriched_id E₁ x₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
      #⊗ (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
          #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₁)
      · (inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₂, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
           (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₁ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₂ x₂
           #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₁ y₂)))

· mon_lunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_runitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V}
  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V I_{ V} (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_lunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_runitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V}
   #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V I_{ V} (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · mon_lunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ mon_runitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)) =
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat

sym_mon_braiding V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V}
#⊗ sym_mon_braiding V I_{ V} (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_lunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_runitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =
mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

 · mon_lunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))
#⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V I_{ V} (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · mon_runitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)) =
mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

 · mon_lunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))
#⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =

#⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

      apply idpath.
  Qed.

   #⊗ identity I_{ V}
   · (identity (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y, F x₂ y ⦄)
      #⊗ enriched_id E₃ (F x₁ y)
      · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y) (F x₁ y) (F x₂ y))) =
(pr121 F) x₁ x₂ y

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y
   #⊗ identity I_{ V}
   · mon_runitor (E₃ ⦃ F x₁ y, F x₂ y ⦄)) =
(pr121 F) x₁ x₂ y

      
V: sym_monoidal_cat

mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
· (mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
   · enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_left F x₁ x₂ y) =
(pr121 F) x₁ x₂ y

      apply id_left.

    · enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)

E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
(mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
 · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂)
#⊗ (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₂ y₂
  #⊗ enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₁ y₁ y₂
· enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂) =
(pr21 F) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
(mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
 · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂)
#⊗ (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· (enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₂ y₂
   #⊗ enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₁ y₁ y₂
   · enriched_comp E₃ (F x₁ y₁) (F x₁ y₂) (F x₂ y₂)) =
(pr21 F) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
(mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
 · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂)
#⊗ (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· (inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₂ ⦄)
     (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂
     #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂
   · enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂) =
(pr21 F) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂

(mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)

    · enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₂ ⦄)
    (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ =

V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category

E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
(mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
 · identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₂ y₂)
#⊗ (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · enriched_id E₁ x₁ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₂, y₂ ⦄)
    (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₁ ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂
· enriched_curried_bifunctor_mor F x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂ =
identity ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· (pr21 F) x₁ x₂ y₁ y₂

x₁, x₂: C₁

inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₁ x₁)
  #⊗ (enriched_id E₂ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))
· enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂

     #⊗ enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂) = ?t2

  #⊗ (enriched_id E₂ y₂ #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ y₁ y₂ y₂) = ?t2

  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ enriched_id E₁ x₁
   · enriched_comp E₁ x₁ x₁ x₂)
  #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) = ?t2

y₁, y₂: C₂
inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
  (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) = ?t2

      apply idpath.
    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (inner_swap V (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) I_{ V} I_{ V}
     (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
   · mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)) =
identity ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· (identity
     ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ I_{ V}
      ⊗ (I_{ V} ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)))
   · mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
     #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)) =
identity ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
· mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
  #⊗ mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =
identity ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
(mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
 · mon_runitor (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄))
#⊗ (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)) =
identity ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄)
#⊗ (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)
    · mon_lunitor (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄)) =
identity ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

    
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
F: enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
x₁, x₂: C₁
y₁, y₂: C₂
identity (E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄) =
identity ((E₁ ⦃ x₁, x₂ ⦄) ⊗ (E₂ ⦃ y₁, y₂ ⦄))

    apply tensor_id_id.
  Qed.
End Inverses.


V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
≃ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃


V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
≃ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
→ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
→ enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
∏ x : enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃,
?g (?f x) = x
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
∏ y : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃,
?f (?g y) = y

  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
→ enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
 exact enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered.
  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
→ enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
 exact enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried.
  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
∏ x : enriched_curried_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃,
enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried
  (enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered x) = x
 exact enriched_whiskered_weq_curried_bifunctor_right.
  
V: sym_monoidal_cat
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
E₃: enrichment C₃ V
∏ y : enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃,
enriched_curried_bifunctor_whiskered
  (enriched_whiskered_bifunctor_to_curried y) = y
 exact enriched_whiskered_weq_curried_bifunctor_left.
Defined.

Definition enriched_bifunctor_whiskered_bifunctor_weq
           {V : sym_monoidal_cat}
           {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
           (E₁ : enrichment C₁ V)
           (E₂ : enrichment C₂ V)
           (E₃ : enrichment C₃ V)
  : enriched_functor
      (tensor_enriched_precat E₁ E₂)
      (make_enriched_cat (C₃ ,, E₃))
    ≃
    enriched_whiskered_bifunctor E₁ E₂ E₃
  := (enriched_curried_whiskered_bifunctor_weq E₁ E₂ E₃
        ∘ enriched_bifunctor_curried_bifunctor_weq E₁ E₂ E₃)%weq.
